SRS002999	SRS002999	Caenorhabditis elegans lin-35 L1 RNA sample 1	Caenorhabditis elegans	NCBI Taxonomy	6239	MT10430	lin-35(n745) I.	L1 larva Ce	WBls	WBls:0000024	hermaphrodite	organism	WBbt	WBbt:0007833	  	  	  	For the lin-35(n745) L1s, we grow the strain at 20 deg until majority of animals are gravid.  2) We bleach the worms to collect embryos, then place the embryos in S-basal buffer and incubate at 20 deg overnight to hatch into L1s.  3) We then put the hatched ~7K L1s on each of 5-6 seeded NGM plates at 20 deg, grow ~3 days until gravid again 4) We then bleach the worms for embryos, put the embryos in S-basal and incubate at 20 deg overnight to hatch into starved L1s. 5) We then place all L1s onto one large seeded plate for 4 hours at 25 deg.  6) We then wash off all worms from food and let them digest their ingested food for one hour in S basal 7) We spin down, monitor pellet size, and then add four volumes of Trizol, perform three rounds of freeze/thaw, and submit for RNA isolation. SRS003000	SRS003000	Caenorhabditis elegans L4 male RNA sample 1	Caenorhabditis elegans	NCBI Taxonomy	6239	CB4689	him-8(e1489)IV.	L4 larva Ce	WBls	WBls:0000038	male	organism	WBbt	WBbt:0007833	  	  	  	For the males we 1) grow dpy-28(y1);him-8(e1489) strain at 15 deg until majority of animals are gravid.  2) We bleach the worms to collect embryos, and then place the embryos in S-basal buffer an d incubate at 25 deg over night to hatch the L1s.  3) We then put the hatched L1s on a seeded NGM plate at 25 deg for 30 hours. SRS003005	SRS003005	Caenorhabditis elegans mid-L1 RNA sample 1	Caenorhabditis elegans	NCBI Taxonomy	6239	N2	wild type genotype	L1 larva Ce	WBls	WBls:0000024	hermaphrodite	organism	WBbt	WBbt:0007833	  	  	  	Embryos were collected by bleaching from mixed stage hermaphrodite populations. Run 30K6TAAXX was labeled L1_ce0077_rw007 and had unexpectedly short inserts with sequences reading through to the linker. They took the same size-fractionated DNA and ran it on another gel. Subsequent runs were then labeled as L1_ce0132_rw007. Reads are in read pairs. The _1 files are the forward reads and the _2 files are the reverse reads.
